      *================================================================
      * Rtv Prod Dt Range f/Or RT - Item Transaction Detail  * 
      *================================================================
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    W0RTN   7
      * USER: Initialize routine
      * C4086 RMC 5.5.15 check for zero date
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     WL0276           Date From
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     WL0277           Date To
      * Declare restrictor key work fields
     C           *LIKE     DEFN TRAIC3    WQNB01           Company Number
     C           *LIKE     DEFN TRC4NB    WQNB02           Order Number
      * Define keylist
     C           KRSNB     KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WQNB01           Company Number
     C                     KFLD           WQNB02           Order Number
      * Setup key
     C                     Z-ADDWL0274    WQNB01           Company Number
     C                     Z-ADDWL0275    WQNB02           Order Number
      * Establish starting position
     C           KRSNB     SETLL@B7CPXK                    *
     C           KRSNB     READE@B7CPXK                  90*
      * Data record not found
     C   90                MOVEL'USR0344' W0RTN   7
     C           *IN90     DOWEQ'0'
      * USER: Process Data record
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0237           Production Date
      * CASE: DB1.Production Date is entered
     C           TRELDT    IFNE 0                          *IF
      * Dont adjust if getting Processing Date Range
      * CASE: PAR.Status Flag 4  Y/N is no
     C           WL0278    IFEQ 'N'                        *IF
     C                     Z-ADDTRELDT    YL0237           Production Date
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
      * Adjust if getting slaughter date range
      * Rtv Variety/Rend/Cut  RT - Company Item  * 
      * Move input parameters to subroutine local variables.
     C                     Z-ADDTRAIC3    WL0268           Company Number
     C                     Z-ADDTRHGCD    WL0269           Item Code
     C                     EXSR TYRVGN
      * Move subroutine local variables to output parameters.
     C                     MOVELWL0270    YL0238    P      Variety_Rendere
      * CASE: LCL.Variety/Rendered/Cut is Cut
     C           YL0238    IFEQ 'C'                        *IF
      * RTV Kill Dt w/Prd Dt   RT - Calendar  * 
      * Move input parameters to subroutine local variables.
     C                     Z-ADDTRAIC3    WL0271           Company Number
     C                     Z-ADDTRELDT    WL0272           Post to G_L Dat
     C                     EXSR TZRVGN
      * Move subroutine local variables to output parameters.
     C                     Z-ADDWL0273    YL0237           Kill Date
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     Z-ADDTRELDT    YL0237           Production Date
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Save earliest date   - thats not zero 5.5.15
      * CASE:
      *  - c1OR(c2ANDc3)
      *   |- c1    : PAR.Date From             USR EQ WRK.ZERO
      *   |- c2    : LCL.Production Date LT PAR.Date From             USR
      *   |- c3    : LCL.Production Date is entered
      *   '-
     C                     MOVEL'0'       Y0CX01  1
     C           WL0276    IFEQ WUW0NB                     *IF
     C                     MOVEL'1'       Y0CX01
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           Y0CX01    IFNE '1'                        *IF
     C           YL0237    IFLT WL0276                     *IF
     C           YL0237    IFNE 0                          *IF
     C                     MOVEL'1'       Y0CX01
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           Y0CX01    IFEQ '1'                        *IF
     C                     Z-ADDYL0237    WL0276           Date From
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Save latest date
      * CASE: LCL.Production Date GT PAR.Date To               USR
     C           YL0237    IFGT WL0277                     *IF
     C                     Z-ADDYL0237    WL0277           Date To
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           KRSNB     READE@B7CPXK                  90*
     C                     ENDDO

      * Convert internal to external date format
      *================================================================
      * Map according to date format
     C                     Z-ADD0         XDEX01           CC
     C           XDDTFM    IFEQ 'DMY'
     C                     Z-ADDXDINDD    XDEX02           DD
     C                     Z-ADDXDINMM    XDEX03           MM
     C                     Z-ADDXDINYY    XDEX04           YY
     C                     ELSE

     C                     Z-ADDXDINMM    XDEX02           MM
     C                     Z-ADDXDINDD    XDEX03           DD
     C                     Z-ADDXDINYY    XDEX04           YY
     C                     ELSE
      * YMD format
     C                     Z-ADDXDINYY    XDEX02           YY
     C                     Z-ADDXDINMM    XDEX03           MM
     C                     Z-ADDXDINDD    XDEX04           DD
     C                     END
     C                     END

      *================================================================
      * Send message to program's message queue
      *================================================================
     C           ZAPGMQ    IFEQ *BLANK
     C                     MOVEL##PGM     ZAPGMQ
     C                     END
      * If no message file specified, use default
     C           ZAMSGF    IFEQ *BLANK
     C                     MOVELZADFMF    ZAMSGF
     C                     END
     C                     CALL 'Y2SNMGC'
     C                     PARM           ZAPGMQ 10        Program queue
     C                     PARM           ZAPGRL  5        Rel queue
     C                     PARM           ZAMSID  7        Message ID
     C                     PARM           ZAMSGF 10        Message file
     C                     PARM           ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     PARM           ZAMSTP  7        Message type
      * Clear all fields for default mechanism next time
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    ZAPGMQ
